## dcimCableTerminationsBulkDelete

> dcimCableTerminationsBulkDelete()





### Example

```javascript
import NetBoxApi from 'net_box_api';
let defaultClient = NetBoxApi.ApiClient.instance;
// Configure API key authorization: Bearer
let Bearer = defaultClient.authentications['Bearer'];
Bearer.apiKey = 'YOUR API KEY';
// Uncomment the following line to set a prefix for the API key, e.g. "Token" (defaults to null)
//Bearer.apiKeyPrefix = 'Token';

let apiInstance = new NetBoxApi.DcimApi();
apiInstance.dcimCableTerminationsBulkDelete((error, data, response) => {
  if (error) {
    console.error(error);
  } else {
    console.log('API called successfully.');
  }
});
```

### Parameters

This endpoint does not need any parameter.

### Return type

## dcimConnectedDeviceList

> Device dcimConnectedDeviceList(peerDevice, peerInterface)



This endpoint allows a user to determine what device (if any) is connected to a given peer device and peer interface. This is useful in a situation where a device boots with no configuration, but can detect its neighbors via a protocol such as LLDP. Two query parameters must be included in the request:  * &#x60;peer_device&#x60;: The name of the peer device * &#x60;peer_interface&#x60;: The name of the peer interface

### Example

```javascript
import NetBoxApi from 'net_box_api';
let defaultClient = NetBoxApi.ApiClient.instance;
// Configure API key authorization: Bearer
let Bearer = defaultClient.authentications['Bearer'];
Bearer.apiKey = 'YOUR API KEY';
// Uncomment the following line to set a prefix for the API key, e.g. "Token" (defaults to null)
//Bearer.apiKeyPrefix = 'Token';

let apiInstance = new NetBoxApi.DcimApi();
let peerDevice = "peerDevice_example"; // String | The name of the peer device
let peerInterface = "peerInterface_example"; // String | The name of the peer interface
apiInstance.dcimConnectedDeviceList(peerDevice, peerInterface, (error, data, response) => {
  if (error) {
    console.error(error);
  } else {
    console.log('API called successfully. Returned data: ' + data);
  }
});
```

### Parameters


Name | Type | Description  | Notes
------------- | ------------- | ------------- | -------------
 **peerDevice** | **String**| The name of the peer device | 
 **peerInterface** | **String**| The name of the peer interface | 

### Return type

## dcimDevicesNapalm

> DeviceNAPALM dcimDevicesNapalm(id, method)



Execute a NAPALM method on a Device

### Example

```javascript
import NetBoxApi from 'net_box_api';
let defaultClient = NetBoxApi.ApiClient.instance;
// Configure API key authorization: Bearer
let Bearer = defaultClient.authentications['Bearer'];
Bearer.apiKey = 'YOUR API KEY';
// Uncomment the following line to set a prefix for the API key, e.g. "Token" (defaults to null)
//Bearer.apiKeyPrefix = 'Token';

let apiInstance = new NetBoxApi.DcimApi();
let id = 56; // Number | A unique integer value identifying this device.
let method = "method_example"; // String | 
apiInstance.dcimDevicesNapalm(id, method, (error, data, response) => {
  if (error) {
```
